  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_994b812d-697a-4f97-a167-493888b5f1e2'
      });
    }

As she witnesses everyone important in her life suffering, she's brought to the ultimate choice: will she sacrifice her soul to save the ones she loves?</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer10401234811992062861">Third instalment of the Heavenly Series, Absolution was everything you could have asked for in the last book in the series. Jennifer wraps up the series with an ending that is heartfelt, filling and completely satisfying. Absolution is the perfect end to a fantastic trilogy.<br/>Zoe still fights Albert for her soul..Her brother knows her secert and her boyfriend to and Albert constantly challenges Zoes will to survive and protect the ones she loves without giving in, her will is challenged, her fight</span>
  <span id="freeText10401234811992062861" style="display:none">Third instalment of the Heavenly Series, Absolution was everything you could have asked for in the last book in the series. Jennifer wraps up the series with an ending that is heartfelt, filling and completely satisfying. Absolution is the perfect end to a fantastic trilogy.<br />Zoe still fights Albert for her soul..Her brother knows her secert and her boyfriend to and Albert constantly challenges Zoes will to survive and protect the ones she loves without giving in, her will is challenged, her fight for survial is challenged but good does conquer over all. Matthias is also faced with certain decisions to make. <br />Albert threatens everyone Zoe loves in her life, she must decide ... <br />I must say I was sad to see this series come to and end, but am very happy with the storyline and final ending. Reading this series Of books I have come to understand love between families with disabilities how hard it must be,can be and I really had no idea . I think knowing that Jennifer has input parts of her life into her books, is very touching and makes the story somewhat very real, and very touching, tissues a must for this book, for the whole series.. I enjoyed the characters in which Jennifer established and I must say the ending was perfect for all. Im sad to see this come to and end, but Im sure Jennifer has more instore for her fans. <br />Recomened to everyone you will be Ab-sol-utely intrigued !!! </span>

  <span id="freeText9895193510947940424" style="display:none">Slightly pissed about this book. Heavenly and Penitence were great- I loved them. Absolution left me confused, which is not a good way to end a series. I was annoyed that it seemed like there was still so much that needed explanation. Matthias had very little appearances, Albert was too easily dismissed, Abria is left without a guardian, Zoe never chose between Weston and Matthias- the only reason she was left with Weston was because Matthias chose to leave- BUT is apparently waiting for her? So where does that leave Weston in the afterlife? I feel sorry for his character, she half-assed their relationship throughout Penitence and Absolution and thats exactly how it stayed til the end of the series when she left Weston in the middle of a dance to go see Matthias. Nothing felt resolved to me.</span>

<div id="review_125734340" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/125734340" />
    <a title="Mindy/fangedmom" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2391157-mindy-fangedmom"><img alt="Mindy/fangedmom" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1294671899p2/2391157.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/125734340?book_show_action=true">Oct 11, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mindy/fangedmom" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mindy/fangedmom" href="/user/show/2391157-mindy-fangedmom">Mindy/fangedmom</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2391157-mindy-fangedmom?shelf=author-sent-autographed">author-sent-autographed</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer125734340" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6624137501994862730">I have been putting off reading this book for quite some time. If I love this series so much, why on EARTH would I put off buying and reading what could be the final book of the HEAVENLY series? That is very simple. I DO NOT WANT THIS SERIES TO EVER END. Seriously. I have fallen in love with this series. Jennifer Laurens has created a story that seems so real to me. Good VS Evil will always prevail in our world. It is a universal symbol. Jennifer has taken Good vs Evil to a whole new level. The </span>
  <span id="freeText6624137501994862730" style="display:none">I have been putting off reading this book for quite some time. If I love this series so much, why on EARTH would I put off buying and reading what could be the final book of the HEAVENLY series? That is very simple. I DO NOT WANT THIS SERIES TO EVER END. Seriously. I have fallen in love with this series. Jennifer Laurens has created a story that seems so real to me. Good VS Evil will always prevail in our world. It is a universal symbol. Jennifer has taken Good vs Evil to a whole new level. The characters are so real. The story unfolds in your mind like a past memory or past life. <br /><br />In book #3, Absolution, we find Zoe still caught up in the battle between good and evil. Zoe has learned a lot over the last two books. She has not only grown up but has also realized how important her family is to her. She realizes that by putting her family first, the shift in balance of good has a lot of weight. She is still in a desperate fight to hang on to her love for Matthias while trying to live her human life too. Zoe and her brother Luke have been through hell and back. Each fighting their own demons. Together, brother and sister have found some common ground. United they sure stand. LOVE this about the story. LOVE LOVE LOVE it. <br /><br />In the end, will love prevail? Will the Heavens be able to contain Matthias or keep Zoe out when demons and dark forces are hell bent on getting her out of the human world? Will Zoe find the life balance she so desperately needs to live out her human existence or will she find a way to be with Matthias? <br /><br />Guess you better get to reading because my reviews are SPOILER FREE! </span>

          </span>

<div id="review_153557847" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/153557847" />
    <a title="Jenna" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3794636-jenna"><img alt="Jenna" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1387634058p2/3794636.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/153557847?book_show_action=true">Mar 10, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jenna" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jenna" href="/user/show/3794636-jenna">Jenna</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer153557847" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2272145374178703761">Absolution. Absolutely full of varieties. Everything was so mixed up. Human emotions crammed with heavenly light. Imagine that.<br/>The book started where "Penitence" (the second book) left off. There were a some things I didn't like about the book but there were also tons of things I loved about it.<br/>First off, the things I loved about it. I liked how Zoe decided to fight off evil and protect her family against it..and in the end, she found herself being honest with them and shared what she saw and ev</span>
  <span id="freeText2272145374178703761" style="display:none">Absolution. Absolutely full of varieties. Everything was so mixed up. Human emotions crammed with heavenly light. Imagine that.<br />The book started where "Penitence" (the second book) left off. There were a some things I didn't like about the book but there were also tons of things I loved about it.<br />First off, the things I loved about it. I liked how Zoe decided to fight off evil and protect her family against it..and in the end, she found herself being honest with them and shared what she saw and everything, and this, made them closer than ever. I like how Jennifer Laurens wrote in a manner that made you feel what the character is feeling too. Whenever Zoe, Weston, Zoe's mom and dad, Luke felt angry, etc. I also feel that same anger. Dealing with temptations..Anyway, because of that the book taught readers to value your family. How you work out the trust, love and understanding in your family. They all love Abria, their autistic sibling and cared for her no matter what. It also touched the subject of abuse in ones family, and I think it was great Jennifer Laurens did it because the book not only focused on one aspect of the truth of family problems. It's not all arguments, but abuse also happens. Because she mentioned this in her story, it only made the message that we should be thankful of what family we are in. I mean, it did to me, as Zoe felt it too.<br /> Another thing I liked about the book was that it's not all about romantic love, but the book showed all sorts of LOVE. Agape love from God, love for your 'rents, and the romantic love we all love to hear. I liked how the book showed how disgusting evil is that you want to destroy it before it reaches you. It seems like it wants to make you want to see evil that way so that when its lurking around you, you can feel it and this pushes you to control your emotions and decisions. Whew! <br />What I didn't like was only this: the fact that she loves Matthias, and Weston. Was it possible to love two people? and the ending was unbelievable. But personally, I liked it because it justifies everything. What I think was Matthias came into her life for a reason-to make her realize the importance of life, love more, and also for Matthias' benefit..for his father to realize that good always prevails..that all of this was to lead Matthias to realize some things too... sacrificing your own happiness will save others...<br /><br />Just like Zoe, I don't like the saying "Everything will work out on itself", but like her, I also find myself saying that now. In this book, many things worked out. Every character wasn't left out lying on the seams. Britt was taken cared off as she's on rehab. There was justice brought on Krissy's life, her parents were on jail and she's under a very caring aunt. Bret was still recuperating with his own soul I guess. Albert was a changed soul-for the good. Luke didn't relapse anymore. Zoe's dad and mom were ok and brought Abria to a conference for better treatment. Weston was a super changed soul too. Zoe changed too. From being a party-goer, popular girl to a good daughter/sister, caring and loving person.<br /><br />I KNOW I WROTE A LOT, AND IT SEEMS LIKE A REFLECTION PAPER TO YOU. BUT THE BOOK WAS WORTH READING FOR ALL THE LESSONS IT GAVE ME. IN ONE SENTENCE: THINGS HAPPEN FOR A REASON, THOUGH WE UNDERGO TEMPTATIONS AND SEEMING ENDLESS TRIALS, BUT IN THE END WE KNOW ITS WORTH STICKING TO THE GOOD..(:</span>
  <a data-text-id="2272145374178703761" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_173662531" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/173662531" />
    <a title="Tasha" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4272116-tasha"><img alt="Tasha" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1339382547p2/4272116.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/173662531?book_show_action=true">Jun 04, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tasha" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tasha" href="/user/show/4272116-tasha">Tasha</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/9473297-absolution">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer173662531&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer173662531" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4887118116394042608">Ok, where to start? Let's start by saying "wow! What a concept!" great story, and I loved the characters! But I have a lot of questions unanswered such as: did I miss why Matthias was assigned to Abria in the first place? What's up with the random changes, Luke was 2 younger in first book then in last book only a year?!? And Abria is 5, yet they are always holding her like a toddler? Maybe thats one source of their problems...just sayin'. And Zoe was responsible for getting her off the bus, she </span>

Zoe was said to have 1st period off from school (which is how she had her 1st convo. with Matthias), then she started going to school the same time as Luke? Did Zoe keep her powers in the end? Great story just a few holes unfilled. </span>

<div id="review_128919995" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/128919995" />
    <a title="Emma " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3342102-emma"><img alt="Emma " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1586199150p2/3342102.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/128919995?book_show_action=true">Nov 02, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Emma " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Emma " href="/user/show/3342102-emma">Emma </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer128919995" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8713454006831655238">I honestly don't know where to start with this one. For some reason I always find it really difficult to write reviews for Jennifer's Heavenly series. It made me think as to why I have such trouble expressing my opinion about these books. If you have read my reviews of Heavenly and Penitence, you will see that this series has touched me on a very personal level and I think that is the reason I stumble when I am writing the reviews. it makes me feel like I am exposing my 'soul' so to speak. I can</span>
  <span id="freeText8713454006831655238" style="display:none">I honestly don't know where to start with this one. For some reason I always find it really difficult to write reviews for Jennifer's Heavenly series. It made me think as to why I have such trouble expressing my opinion about these books. If you have read my reviews of Heavenly and Penitence, you will see that this series has touched me on a very personal level and I think that is the reason I stumble when I am writing the reviews. it makes me feel like I am exposing my 'soul' so to speak. I can relate to most of the characters in one way or another:<br /><br />Mrs Dodd (Zoe's Mother): her internal struggle about putting her autistic daughter first and the effect it has on the other children. If you remember my oldest child is dyspraxic and she tends to be the one that gets the main focus of attention, which does make me worry about the emotional health of the other two girls. It is emotionally and physically draining at times. Adding to the strain on other relationships.<br /><br />Zoe: following her epiphany in Heavenly, Zoe manages to alter the course of her life for the better. Gain inner strength, faith and contentment most of us strive our whole lives to achieve. Her ability to find forgiveness and emotional restraint against all negative emotions is enviable.<br /><br />Luke: (Zoe's Brother) tries to escape from the reality of his life by the use of drugs. Again I can relate, not with the drugs but in our family case alcohol is the poison of choice. I have witnessed the struggle and daily temptation that addiction can bring. Seeing Luke overcome his addiction with the strength that Zoe's belief in him provides.<br /><br />Mr Dodd (Zoe's father) the strain both emotionally, physically and financially all take its toll. The way in which the family bonds are shown as a united entity is inspiring.<br /><br />Absolution starts at the exact point that Penitence ended plunging the reader into the action from the start. This is a series that you have to read in order to fully appreciate the storyline. Although there is brilliant recapping of pivotal plot points skilfully interwoven into the current plot.<br /><br />The darker side of life is shown in terrifying vividness with the ghastly black evil spirits so easy to conjure within the imagination and truly frightening. It is easy to picture them at times of intense negative emotions. Zoe's ability to control her emotions and negate negativity is truly awe inspiring. Something that is not easy to do yet is something that more of us should try to achieve (especially me).<br /><br />The way in which friendship, family and love are portrayed, and their ability to enhance our lives for the better is beautiful. Daily life is not easy, and it is hard to remember to count the blessings we have no matter how small. This series always makes me do that, stand back and be grateful for the little things. No matter how tough things get, you have to have faith. As I have continually stated I am not overtly religious but the whole ethos of having faith in something and positive thinking while avoiding negativity is something I can appreciate.<br /><br />The characters development throughout the narrative was wonderful, all of them progressed and developed as separate individuals yet remained as a core unit. Even Abria's development was a pleasure to witness. Most surprisingly for me was the way I felt about Weston through this book. Previously I resented him being with Zoe as I felt he was coming between her and Matthias. However, through his development within this story I actually found myself appreciating the relationship he has with Zoe, not perfect being human and all, he really does strife to be like Zoe with his positivity and avoiding the negative. <br /><br />As much as I wanted to make Mathias human or Zoe an angel so that they could be together. I have to say the ending was PERFECT just ab-sol-utely perfect. I cried my eyes out with big gulping sobs, so even J noticed. I couldn't speak for ages after closing the last page for fear of bursting into yet more tears but it was still PERFECT.<br /><br />To round off I just want to say that for me this is a comfort read. It gives me hope like a ray of sunshine in my life. It came into my life at a crucial point and for that I will be eternally grateful to Jennifer. If you know me then you will realise I tend to say that 'reading is subjective' quite a lot, in fact I am going to make it my catchphrase [: D] That is how I view the Heavenly series for me they are completely personal, I relate to them from my own experiences, they have helped me come to terms with some things and for that I adore them and Jennifer for writing them and sharing them with me</span>
  <a data-text-id="8713454006831655238" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer171525002" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9781282793633315858">I have been pondering on what I could say for Absolution that I haven’t already said about the other two books for a week now. I have drawn the conclusion to keep it real and share how it has made me look differently on life. For me this is so much more than being a love story it is more of a message on how you should treat others and live your life. I feel like Jennifer Laurens sends a huge message to her readers and I hope everyone can take what I did from these three beautifully written books</span>
  <span id="freeText9781282793633315858" style="display:none">I have been pondering on what I could say for Absolution that I haven’t already said about the other two books for a week now. I have drawn the conclusion to keep it real and share how it has made me look differently on life. For me this is so much more than being a love story it is more of a message on how you should treat others and live your life. I feel like Jennifer Laurens sends a huge message to her readers and I hope everyone can take what I did from these three beautifully written books.<br /><br />Now……….. with all of this being said and me exposing my soul here this is by far my favorite of the three. The book is very fast paced, so many loose ends are tied up and new things arise. I felt like with each new page something different was happening. All the while Zoe stays as strong and incredible as always.<br /><br />I found in this book you really had an opportunity to learn about the secondary characters. It was nice to see them developed and for more of their stories to be told. I will say I loved the direction Luke’s character took. I felt like he too became a very strong young man like his sister Zoe.<br /><br />Well I am not going to gush any longer about this book. I hope that you make the choice to read this series. Like many books there are slow areas however once you get through them it is so worth it. Jennifer Laurens has created three beautiful books and for her I am grateful. My only complaint is it is over. I will miss the family very much and they will always hold a dear place in my heart.<br /></span>

           <span class="uitext reviewText">all my Paranormal/fantasy readers</span></div>

<div id="review_102623750" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/102623750" />
    <a title="Lynsey" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2894074-lynsey"><img alt="Lynsey" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1269872280p2/2894074.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/102623750?book_show_action=true">May 13, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lynsey" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lynsey" href="/user/show/2894074-lynsey">Lynsey</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer102623750" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17652538217875977043">Anyone that knows me in the blogosphere knows that I am a HUGE fan of Jennifer Lauren’s books and so to say I was eager to read Absolution, the final book in the Heavenly series, is an understatement at best. I feel honoured to have read this before the publication date and guys, believe me when I tell you that you will not be disappointed. Before I go any further, if you have NOT yet read Heavenly and the most awesome sequel ever Penitence then...1. Where have you been? 2. You are SERIOUSLY mis</span>
  <span id="freeText17652538217875977043" style="display:none">Anyone that knows me in the blogosphere knows that I am a HUGE fan of Jennifer Lauren’s books and so to say I was eager to read Absolution, the final book in the Heavenly series, is an understatement at best. I feel honoured to have read this before the publication date and guys, believe me when I tell you that you will not be disappointed. Before I go any further, if you have NOT yet read Heavenly and the most awesome sequel ever Penitence then...1. Where have you been? 2. You are SERIOUSLY missing out and 3. Go read them RIGHT. NOW!<br /><br />I read this book in a day. I started it early afternoon, had to stop so I could go and have a social life (even though all I wanted to do was read the book) and then started again at midnight when I came home! I finished it at 4am. I was only supposed to read until 2am but then I kept making deals with myself – ok 2 30am, 3am and that’s final, oh alright 3 30am then suddenly it was 4am! Jennifer managed to do what Claudia Gray did in Hourglass which was to write something so compelling at the end of each chapter that just MADE me have to read on. When I finished reading the last book, Penitence, I predicted that there were going to be some major tears for this book and...I was right. Tears were STREAMING down my face and unfortunately I was still wearing mascara. NON WATERPROOF. When I caught a look at myself in the mirror I looked a complete mess! But it was sooooo worth it.<br /><br />Absolution literally picks up where Penitence leaves off. Krissy is having a tough time at home after Brady’s funeral and finds solace in an unlikely hero. Luke is still battling his own demons and Britt is on the brink of destroying herself. Weston doesn’t know whether he can handle everything that’s going on with him and Zoe, especially now he knows her secret. And what will he do when he finds out about Matthias? Matthias is trying to stand back a little but is still there when Zoe is in dire need which is more and more frequent as Albert is intent on tearing Zoe’s family apart so that she will give into his desire for her soul. OH. MY. GOODNESS. people. The final book in the Heavenly series is definitely the darker of the three, there’s a lot of tension coming from all angles and Zoe is bang smack in the middle of everything.<br /><br />I think I love each and every one of the characters in this series. Zoe has such a mature and distinctive voice, she’s definitely grown over the three books and I’ve enjoyed sharing the journey with her. Like Zoe, I’m IN LOVE with both Weston and Matthias, I mean how can a girl possibly choose between them?!?!? I also hold a special little place in my heart for Luke, possibly because I’ve always wanted a little brother and I want to save him from himself.<br /><br />I like the fact that in this book, we find out a lot more about Krissy, even if her back story is less than ideal. And Chase remains one of my favourite minor characters. I love the fact that Zoe has never ditched their regular Starbucks outings just because she has a boyfriend, proving that just because you’re in a relationship, it doesn’t mean you have to ditch your friends.<br /><br />Abria is a little sweetheart and has taught us a lot more about autism and what it’s like to live with a child who has the condition. It can he embarrassing, heartbreaking, tiring but also rewarding and a relationship full of love.<br /><br />Overall, this was an excellent ending to one of the best series’ I’ve ever read and enjoyed. I was definitely sad for it to end and will miss Matthias more than I thought I would. I would love to see a spin off series or short story involving all the same characters. Ideally of course, another book would be good but I’m not sure that’s going to happen. I may just have to seek out or even write some fan fiction just so I can get my Matthias fix!<br /><br />Whilst there is a sense of resolve to the story and absolution is definitely a fitting title, it is ever so slightly deceiving because not everything is absolute ;) If you don’t know what I’m going on about, you will understand when you’ve read the book. If I had a rating system, this would get five stars out of five and even more, if possible. Absolution is a compelling read that will take your breath away and I can’t recommend it highly enough.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17652538217875977043" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_112617162" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/112617162" />
    <a title="Aileen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2206485-aileen"><img alt="Aileen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1270570733p2/2206485.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/112617162?book_show_action=true">Jul 20, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aileen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aileen" href="/user/show/2206485-aileen">Aileen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2206485-aileen?shelf=own">own</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer112617162" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11560357720597570350">When I first started this series with Heavenly I fell in love with this series as much as Zoe fell in love with Matthias. I waited and waited and read Penitence, then I waited and waited some more and read Absolution. The first thing I can say about Absolution is that I have never cried over a book a few days later just THINKING about the book, until I finished Absolution. I can also say that the Heavenly series is the only one that I know EVERYONE I suggest it too will LOVE it the way I do. I r</span>
  <span id="freeText11560357720597570350" style="display:none">When I first started this series with Heavenly I fell in love with this series as much as Zoe fell in love with Matthias. I waited and waited and read Penitence, then I waited and waited some more and read Absolution. The first thing I can say about Absolution is that I have never cried over a book a few days later just THINKING about the book, until I finished Absolution. I can also say that the Heavenly series is the only one that I know EVERYONE I suggest it too will LOVE it the way I do. I read this book the day I got it and ever since then every time I even THINK about it, I want to burst into tears and read it all over again. It was one of the best books I have ever read. The love between Zoe and Matthias is the most pure, most holy, most beautiful love story I have ever read, and will read. I don't think that any story can top the story of Matthias and Zoe. I believe that is why it was so hard to read the end of it and to write what I thought of it. In the start of Absolution you know that Albert, Matthias' father, Albert, is still trying to capture both Zoe and Matthias' soul, even though Matthias is his own son. You know that Weston is in love with Zoe and Zoe loves Weston, but she also loves Matthias. You also know that Zoe has told her brother and Weston about Matthias and while her brother Luke can handle it, and can even see him, Weston cannot see him but he knows that Zoe is in love with him and he doesn't like it. He wants Zoe for himself, this makes him susceptible to Albert and Weston's old, now dead, best friend Brady, and allows them to try to make him turn on Zoe and try to make her do things she doesn't want to do. This is just the beginning of one of the greatest books I have ever read. This story goes on with ups and downs and it makes you a little bit crazy with each passing page because you know that there will be a point where Zoe has to make a choice. She has to choose between Heaven and Earth. She has to choose between the angel who she loves, and the mortal who loves her. She loves both Matthias and Weston, but she can't have both of them, at least not at once. Then you have Albert, who is bent on stealing Matthias' soul and will use Zoe to get it. Albert uses everything he can to get Zoe, like telling her bits and pieces about Matthias' past, whether they are true or not. But in Absolution Zoe will face an even harder challenge. She has to face letting go of the one she loves, but the true question that you have all the while reading this book is...who will it be?? Will it be Matthias, the guardian angel who Zoe loves so deep she feels it in her soul?? Or will it be Weston, the mortal, who accepts that Zoe sees both good and bad spirits and still loves her for all her imperfections?? All I can say is that no matter who chooses to keep, and who she chooses to let go...it will be a heartbreaking decision either way and it will keep you on edge from beginning to end. It will also keep you crying your eyes out until you are blue in the face and sick of being sad over it, since the ending is still happy in it's own way. This book deserves MORE then just five stars, and if I could stand crying every time I would read it over and over because it is just the most perfect love story I have ever read.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11560357720597570350" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_107092178" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/107092178" />
    <a title="Melissa Silva" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3237000-melissa-silva"><img alt="Melissa Silva" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1322792959p2/3237000.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/107092178?book_show_action=true">Jun 14, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melissa Silva" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melissa Silva" href="/user/show/3237000-melissa-silva">Melissa Silva</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer107092178" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6100962138761998497">Absolution is the third book in Jennifer Laurens Heavenly Series. I've been waiting anxiously to read this book and let me tell you I was not disappointed, it was everything I expected and more.<br/><br/>WARNING THERE ARE SPOILERS, ESPECIALLY FOR THOSE WHO HAVE NOT READ ANY BOOK IN THE SERIES YET!****CAUTION*****<br/><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/>Absolution takes place right after Brady's funeral. Zoe is still being haunted by Albert and he is doing everything he can to ruin her life by attacking her family with his evil pressence. The sli</span>
  <span id="freeText6100962138761998497" style="display:none">Absolution is the third book in Jennifer Laurens Heavenly Series. I've been waiting anxiously to read this book and let me tell you I was not disappointed, it was everything I expected and more.<br /><br />WARNING THERE ARE SPOILERS, ESPECIALLY FOR THOSE WHO HAVE NOT READ ANY BOOK IN THE SERIES YET!****CAUTION*****<br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br />Absolution takes place right after Brady's funeral. Zoe is still being haunted by Albert and he is doing everything he can to ruin her life by attacking her family with his evil pressence. The slightest argument gets blown up into a frenzy of emotions and he will not settle on just her family but everyone who is close to her just to get Matthias' soul. <br /><br />Nerves are worn thin and trying to get back into the swing of things is becoming very difficult. Krissy is filled with guilt over her disaster of a party and with her dad a raging maniac threatening everyone he can think of to find his daughter after she ran away things become a bit complicated. Luke finds her hitchiking and becomes surprisingly close to her in order to comfort her, finding out truths about her life that make Zoe and Luke feel horrible and trying to do anything they can to find a way to help her. Zoe knows there is something wrong with Krissy's father because of the swarm of black spirits latched on to him.<br /><br />Albert's attempt to destroy her family has put a strain on Zoe and because of him she is forced to tell her parents the truth about everything, from her 'near death' experience and about Matthias. Albert's influence on everyone has made Zoe's life very stressful and it doesn't help matters when Brady's influence is focused on Weston. His short fuse makes it even more difficult for Weston to keep his cool and when he turns his aggression on Zoe, she is pushed into a situation where she must keep Weston calm and explain to him that he feels this way because of Brady wrapping his evil tendrils around him. It becomes easier for Weston to handle the idea of his former best friend pushing him to the edge of darkness when Matthias finally reveals himself to Weston.<br /><br />The ending of Absolution is Ab-So-Lute-Ly Fantastic! An unexpected outcome involving Albert makes your heart swell with joy and the heartbreakingly beautiful ending makes you never want it to end. But life goes on as Zoe realizes and Matthias becomes more important to the world then she can even imagine.<br /><br />Jennifer Laurens' Heavenly series is a MUST READ, Absolution is a great conclusion to this trilogy and I can only hope to read more in the future but if this is truely the end I am happy :) Thanks to Jennifer for creating such a wonderful and heart-warming series and for being such a great writer AND friend.<br /><br /><br />Melissa Silva<br />The Bookshelf</span>
  <a data-text-id="6100962138761998497" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_329451218" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/329451218" />
    <a title="Stacia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5762917-stacia"><img alt="Stacia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1339655731p2/5762917.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/329451218?book_show_action=true">May 13, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacia" href="/user/show/5762917-stacia">Stacia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Romance-Lovers, Angel-Lovers</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5762917-stacia?shelf=re-read">re-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer329451218&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer329451218" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16343812814748011580"><i> 4 out of 5 stars! </i><br/>What a fine way to end a trilogy. I was absolutely blown away by <i> Absolution </i> by <b> Laurens. </b> <br/><br/>Anyone who looks through my shelves, or even just glances at my profile can see I absolutely <b> love </b> angel books. Something about a celestial being that has always been portrayed as Divine and Righteous, falling for a human, is just so... magical and beautiful to me. And written like <b> Laurens </b> graced us with, I could say the trilogy goes down as one of my favorites.<br/><br/>Zoe's secret is reveal</span>
  <span id="freeText16343812814748011580" style="display:none"><i> 4 out of 5 stars! </i><br />What a fine way to end a trilogy. I was absolutely blown away by <i> Absolution </i> by <b> Laurens. </b> <br /><br />Anyone who looks through my shelves, or even just glances at my profile can see I absolutely <b> love </b> angel books. Something about a celestial being that has always been portrayed as Divine and Righteous, falling for a human, is just so... magical and beautiful to me. And written like <b> Laurens </b> graced us with, I could say the trilogy goes down as one of my favorites.<br /><br />Zoe's secret is revealed left and right in this book. To the most unsuspecting figures. Her brother, Luke, Her boyfriend, Weston (who coincidentally used to be her ex-best friend's boyfriend) knows her secret and claims he can't live without Zoe. Her parents know, hesitant at first, but soon wrap their minds around the idea.<br /><br />And while <b> Laurens </b> doesn't spend much time on forming a bond between Matthais and Zoe's parents like I would have hoped for, she does make an effort to make a connection between Luke and Matthais, and while it wasn't as deep as I would have liked, it was something.<br /><br />And the relationship between Weston and Zoe is... strange, at first, because I had a deep hatred for Weston after the party. Who wouldn't? How dare he attempt to hurt Zoe! <br /><br />While Zoe is getting used to the idea of Weston in her life, over Matthais, she also has to deal with Albert, an unlikely figure reeking havoc on Zoe and every aspect of her life- he influences Zoe's parents to fight about the smallest things, and influences Luke into using again. The only weapon at Zoe's disposal is her little sister, Abria, who is autistic, and therefore considered an Innocent in the eyes of the Light.<br /><br />Throw all of this in the mix with Britt, Zoe's best friend, who wants nothing more than to get back with Weston, who wants nothing to do with her. Chase, Zoe's editor-in-chief friend who wants Zoe. And Krissy, who wants Weston, at first, has a fling with Chase, then ultimately sinks her claws into Luke, after he falls for her while she is living a fearful situation.<br /><br />Zoe and Matthais have heartfelt conversations. Really, they ripped my heart out, at times.<br /><br />Ultimately, <i> Absolution </i> was a mix of tears and rage. There were many times I had to sit the book down, and walk away because of the frustration of not being able to read it fast enough. It was a beautiful and fitting end, and I wouldn't have it any other way. I'm glad <b> Laurens </b> ended it the way she did. <br /><br />This is a series that I will be pulling from my shelves, repeatedly, for many years to come.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16343812814748011580" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_128096047" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/128096047" />
    <a title="Laura" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4468241-laura"><img alt="Laura" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1326933462p2/4468241.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/128096047?book_show_action=true">Oct 27, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laura" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laura" href="/user/show/4468241-laura">Laura</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4468241-laura?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4468241-laura?shelf=angels">angels</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer128096047&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer128096047" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13593468237728700671">"Absolution is a traditional theological term for the forgiveness experienced in the Sacrament of Reconciliation. This concept is found in the Catholic Church, as well as the Eastern Orthodox churches, the Anglican Communion, and Lutheranism." - Wikipedia. <br/><br/>Basically ABSOLUTION (the book) is everything it's wrapped up to be. All the characters in this series, that seek redemption of any kind are on the road to it. Weather they receive it, find their way to it, decide upon it, etc- it's for each p</span>
  <span id="freeText13593468237728700671" style="display:none">"Absolution is a traditional theological term for the forgiveness experienced in the Sacrament of Reconciliation. This concept is found in the Catholic Church, as well as the Eastern Orthodox churches, the Anglican Communion, and Lutheranism." - Wikipedia. <br /><br />Basically ABSOLUTION (the book) is everything it's wrapped up to be. All the characters in this series, that seek redemption of any kind are on the road to it. Weather they receive it, find their way to it, decide upon it, etc- it's for each person/ entity. <br /><br />It basically takes off right where PENITENCE (Book #2) leaves off. What is amazing to really see here is how much the main character of Zoe has changed since HEAVENLY (Book #1). She's such a fierce, kick ass character. Someone who is no longer a victim to her own issues and is willing to fight for herself and those she loves. <br /><br />Zoe has two loves in this book which makes things a bit complicated for her. She loves her guardian Angel Matthias eternally- he's the one for her, her soul mate. But he's also an Angel who lives and dwells in the Heavens. However, it is Matthias' prophecy that they will be "together one day." He's known this since the day he met Zoe. <br /><br />Zoe also loves mortal Westin. She loves him enough to be with him on Earth. He's a loving, warm, comforting presence for her. He's a safe companion for her, as Matthias has told her. <br /><br />So what will happen? Who will she end up with, how will it go down? <br /><br />She's also being hunted by Matthias' father Albet who is evil and will stop at nothing to bring down Matthias and will use Zoe to do so. But Zoe is stronger now and is learning how to defend herself against evil forces. However, Matthias is not happy at all that Zoe is in the middle and would almost rather sacrifice himself to keep her safe. <br /><br />The ending of this novel is quite different than how most YA paranormal romance novels I've read end. Or at least if it ended this way, there would be another book to keep it going. It's not a cliffhanger, but it's got the effect of the bittersweet reality we live in. The reality I have lived in for a while now. <br /><br />I thoroughly enjoyed this series. And although it was a bit juvenile at times and maybe a bit preachy as well, the entire story and point of it as a whole was enjoyable and had something to say and meant something. I very much recommend it!</span>
  <a data-text-id="13593468237728700671" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer775308703" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5662874319859340459">This book left me with one emotion-irritation. Now don't get me wrong here. I loved the first two books Heavenly and Penitence. What happened with this one? <br/>1. First of all, Zoe-make up your mind! Zoe is apparently dating Weston, but is also still in love with Matthias. The only reason shes with Weston is because Matthias told her to move on and live her life. Okay, I understand. But every time Weston was kissing her or they were having an intimate scene, Zoe was thinking of Matthias. If you lov</span>
  <span id="freeText5662874319859340459" style="display:none">This book left me with one emotion-irritation. Now don't get me wrong here. I loved the first two books Heavenly and Penitence. What happened with this one? <br />1. First of all, Zoe-make up your mind! Zoe is apparently dating Weston, but is also still in love with Matthias. The only reason shes with Weston is because Matthias told her to move on and live her life. Okay, I understand. But every time Weston was kissing her or they were having an intimate scene, Zoe was thinking of Matthias. If you love Matthias leave Weston. Stop thinking about two guys, like one is not enough. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ and then the time they were going to prom. Zoe was worried about Matthias but not enough to stop her from going? She didn't love Matthias enough and she cared more about her prom-which seriously pissed me off  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />2. The second is because of Matthias. I fell in love with Matthias from the beginning of the series and still loved him throughout, but considering that this was the last installment of the series, Matthias was barely in the book. The whole plot was like Zoe and Weston's love story with an occasional Matthias as a third wheel. He was in the beginning, middle, and end. He comes and goes in half a page. <br />3.The plot. The plot was so infuriating. There are two ways this plot can go. 1. Weston and Zoe are making out. Albert comes and tries to take her soul. Zoe thinks of Matthias. Matthias comes and saves her. Zoe tells Matthias she loves him. She goes back to Weston. OR 2.Zoe is about to have sex with Weston. She tells him to stop. Weston is influenced by Brady and hurts Zoe. He comes back to his senses and tells Zoe hes sorry. Zoe forgives him and they make out. <br /> I would recommend this book to anybody who wants a bad finish to a great start of the series. I rarely ever rate books with a one star. I was considering giving this book a no star, but because of Matthias, I generously gave it a star. It was actually a relief that <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ ZOE DOESNT END UP WITH MATTHIAS IN HER MORTAL LIFE  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> because she doesnt deserve a great guy like him. Im going to stop with my rant, and go find another book-A GOOD BOOK-and calm myself. </span>

<div id="review_115443319" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/115443319" />
    <a title="Lisa " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3699439-lisa"><img alt="Lisa " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1364442075p2/3699439.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/115443319?book_show_action=true">Aug 05, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lisa " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lisa " href="/user/show/3699439-lisa">Lisa </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3699439-lisa?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3699439-lisa?shelf=jennifer-laurens">jennifer-laurens</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3699439-lisa?shelf=my-top-picks">my-top-picks</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer115443319" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14211051753258567054">Have you ever had a piece of cake or your favorite pastry, sitting in front of you waiting to be devoured? It looks so delicious and so satisfying that you almost don't want to eat it because then it will be gone. So then you decide to eat it, but instead of shoveling it onto your mouth you take your time, savor each bite. That's what reading this book was like for me. I'll give you another example, since its the holidays I'll use Christmas. When you're a kid, or at least it was always this way </span>
  <span id="freeText14211051753258567054" style="display:none">Have you ever had a piece of cake or your favorite pastry, sitting in front of you waiting to be devoured? It looks so delicious and so satisfying that you almost don't want to eat it because then it will be gone. So then you decide to eat it, but instead of shoveling it onto your mouth you take your time, savor each bite. That's what reading this book was like for me. I'll give you another example, since its the holidays I'll use Christmas. When you're a kid, or at least it was always this way for me, Christmas eve was better then Christmas day. Throughout the whole day on Christmas eve, its great because you have the anticipation of Christmas day to look forward to. But on Christmas day its always a little sad because its over. It took me a long time to read this book, simply because I didn't want the series to end.<br /><br />I fell in love with Matthias from the very first time Zoe met him in the park. He reminded me of Edward from Twilight because he had that mature and wise yet still sexy quality about him. He just like Edward was born in a different time, and as a result saw the present world in a slightly different way. Zoe on the other hand, is nothing like Bella. Zoe is confident and sure of herself and in beginning a bit of a wild child. But I think that's why she fell in love with Matthias. On the surface they are opposites, but their hearts beat the same.<br /><br />So in this third and final installment in the Heavenly series, Zoe comes full circle. I loved it like I loved the first two. All of our questions get answered and in my opinion the author ended things pleasantly. However, Zoe does not get to have her cake and eat it too! Of course if it were up to me the series would continue, but all good things must come to an end I guess. Though I think all the Heavenly fans will agree with me that it's time to campaign for a movie! <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="14211051753258567054" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_131403109" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/131403109" />
    <a title="Brandi Kosiner " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2614253-brandi-kosiner"><img alt="Brandi Kosiner " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1593741913p2/2614253.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/131403109?book_show_action=true">Nov 18, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brandi Kosiner " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brandi Kosiner " href="/user/show/2614253-brandi-kosiner">Brandi Kosiner </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer131403109" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6308798387007252186">I really love the Heavenly series by Jennifer, and this book did not let me down. Absolution had everything that I hoped for and more! It is such a story of hope, repentance, forgiveness, and true love. It not only demonstrates a familial love, working through troubles and coming out stronger, but what love in friendship should be like, as well as romantic love. <br/> Zoe has really matured and blossomed and she deals with everything that bombards her in such a loving and awesome way. I really have g</span>
  <span id="freeText6308798387007252186" style="display:none">I really love the Heavenly series by Jennifer, and this book did not let me down. Absolution had everything that I hoped for and more! It is such a story of hope, repentance, forgiveness, and true love. It not only demonstrates a familial love, working through troubles and coming out stronger, but what love in friendship should be like, as well as romantic love. <br /> Zoe has really matured and blossomed and she deals with everything that bombards her in such a loving and awesome way. I really have grown to love her character and admire her actions. She is not perfect, but she is perfectly written. I love her bravery, and her mouth even though it gets her in trouble occasionally. <br /> Abria is ever present and she continues to teach love, acceptance and tolerance. I adore her character, her innocence, and her complete trust. I also appreciate how she is given a bit of hope in this book while still being realistic to the disease.<br /> Weston is ever handsome and gentlemanly in this book... while he is himself. There are a few scenes that I was not happy with, but I understand why they are written and his actions... if that makes any sense. I really appreciate his love and loyalty to Zoe, even with her conflicted heart. <br /> Matthias is as wonderful as ever in Absolution as well. His character has always been so pure, loving, and he has this non-judgmental way of telling it like it as and how it should be. His faith and steadfast convictions in those he loves really just makes me want to cry, and yearn for that to be directed my way. <br /> Laurens really has written a masterpiece, and I would recommend getting your hands on this book and the series as quickly as you can!</span>
  <a data-text-id="6308798387007252186" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer5129499389340160340">I was so crazy about these books that I read all of them in 3 days. <br/>I loved Matthias in the first 2 books and I really wanted them to find a way to be together... but then something changed and I fell completely in love with Weston. I wanted to grab Zoe by the shoulders and shake her and say "how can you not see how amazing this guy is?", he loves her so much, he's caring, he's awesome and he's real. <br/>In the 3rd book I caught myself rolling my eyes at the Zoe/Matthias scenes, I thought they dragg</span>
  <span id="freeText5129499389340160340" style="display:none">I was so crazy about these books that I read all of them in 3 days. <br />I loved Matthias in the first 2 books and I really wanted them to find a way to be together... but then something changed and I fell completely in love with Weston. I wanted to grab Zoe by the shoulders and shake her and say "how can you not see how amazing this guy is?", he loves her so much, he's caring, he's awesome and he's real. <br />In the 3rd book I caught myself rolling my eyes at the Zoe/Matthias scenes, I thought they dragged a little bit and he wasn't that present. I also felt like Zoe didn't really like Weston that much. When she said she loved him, I didn't really feel it, she just said "love you" ... like "yeah, whatever". She should have said " I love you" like she really meant it (and not over the phone)... I guess she didn't love him, at least that's what I felt. <br />I'm probably a hopeless romantic but I don't think it's fair to Weston that she says she loves him and that she's with him but wanting to be with Matthias. That's kinda sad and selfish. <br />It's still an amazing book and I'm hoping that there's a book #4, maybe then she'll make up her mind and I'm REALLY hoping she'll fall in love with Weston, for real this time :)</span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer10177398540565335482">I’m now a few chapters in. It starts just where Penitence left off, on the day of Brady’s funeral. Zoe and Chase are on their way to Krissy’s house, to talk to Krissy who seemed upset about something. As you may recall from Penitence, Krissy’s father appears to be one evil man, if judged by the many black spirits that constantly encircle his persona. Krissy refuses to tell Zoe what is bothering her, but it I have a strong feeling her father has something to do with it.<br/><br/>Meanwhile, the father of Ma</span>
  <span id="freeText10177398540565335482" style="display:none">I’m now a few chapters in. It starts just where Penitence left off, on the day of Brady’s funeral. Zoe and Chase are on their way to Krissy’s house, to talk to Krissy who seemed upset about something. As you may recall from Penitence, Krissy’s father appears to be one evil man, if judged by the many black spirits that constantly encircle his persona. Krissy refuses to tell Zoe what is bothering her, but it I have a strong feeling her father has something to do with it.<br /><br />Meanwhile, the father of Matthias, the evil Albert, is making Zoe’s family home life a living hell, causing her parents to argue at all times. Will Zoe ever be able to make it stop, and if so, how? She decides to tell her parents the truth about her being able to communicate with spirits. Because if they know that Albert is causing their rages, that may prevent it. Or so she hopes.<br /><br />And this is as far as I’ve got. As usual I have no clue where the plot will take me. It seems as if Krissy will play a bigger part here, but how? Will Weston return again? Please Laurens, make him return! And finally, will Zoe be able to get rid of Albert, and keep Matthias at the same time?<br /><br />So many questions. Can they all be answered in less than 200 pages? I truly hope so!<br /><br />Full review coming soon..</span>

<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/51007311-heart-bones"><img alt="Heart Bones" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1580936060l/51007311._SX98_.jpg" />

<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('vuiRrVVvl6x/GNfTmzyszatXMloyKEDVaEHTextSqU+RWvnZkJsNtj66GGBAfjcgZOCRw0URewqedAqEypFjxA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer16276580392840000850">Jennifer, aka JM Warwick was born and raised in Southern California and her hometown of Palos Verdes Estates flavors her books: A Season of Eden and An Open Vein. She doesn't limit herself to writing one genre, and was the first to author four romance novels centered around the popular sport of ballroom dancing.She has YA novels published under her YA romance name of Jennifer Laurens: Falling for </span>
  <span id="freeText16276580392840000850" style="display:none">Jennifer, aka JM Warwick was born and raised in Southern California and her hometown of Palos Verdes Estates flavors her books: A Season of Eden and An Open Vein. She doesn't limit herself to writing one genre, and was the first to author four romance novels centered around the popular sport of ballroom dancing.She has YA novels published under her YA romance name of Jennifer Laurens: Falling for Romeo, Magic Hands, Nailed and the Heavenly series: Heavenly ( 2009) Penitence (2010) and Absolution (2010) A Season of Eden (2011) and Overprotected ( 2011 ) Grace Doll ( 2012 ) .An Open Vein is under her JM Warwick pen name. Jennifer lives in Utah and has 6 children, one of whom has autism. Jennifer doesn't put stock in reviews - in fact she never reads them.</span>
